<section class="divisions" id="divisions" aria-label="What we're building — divisions">

  <div class="div-panel" id="panelLeft">

    <span class="eyebrow">Magenta Originals</span>

    <h3>What<br>We Own</h3>

    <p>Film, series, and digital properties developed in-house, concept to finished work. AI accelerates development and previs; direction, writing, and judgment stay with our team. This is how MAGENTA builds what it owns.</p>

  </div>

  <div class="div-panel" id="panelRight">

    <span class="eyebrow">Magenta Creative Services</span>

    <h3>What<br>We Make</h3>

    <p>Campaign and commercial production for brands and agencies — pitch to finished deliverable at a pace and cost traditional production can't match, without lowering the ceiling. This division funds the studio.</p>

    <a class="cta" href="#contact" data-anchor>Start a project</a>

/* entry vectors per axis type — always fully off-screen at progress 0 */

function vectors(axis){

  switch(axis){

    case "diag":  return {r:{x:"-85vw",y:"-70vh",rot:-24}, b:{x:"85vw",y:"-70vh",rot:24}};

    case "y":     return {r:{x:"-6vw",y:"110vh",rot:4},    b:{x:"6vw",y:"-110vh",rot:-4}};

    case "scale": return {r:{x:"-85vw",y:0,rot:-60},       b:{x:"85vw",y:0,rot:60}};

    default:      return {r:{x:"-90vw",y:0,rot:0},         b:{x:"90vw",y:0,rot:0}};

  }

}


/* ---------------- build sections ---------------- */

const main = document.getElementById("story");

SECTIONS.forEach((s)=>{

  const sec = document.createElement("section");

  sec.className = "letter-section";

  sec.setAttribute("aria-label", s.eyebrow);

  sec.innerHTML = `

    <div class="bg-depth lm-anchor" aria-hidden="true" style="aspect-ratio:auto">

      <div class="d r lm-${s.asset}"></div>

      <div class="d b lm-${s.asset}"></div>

    </div>

    <div class="merge">

      <div class="glyph r lm-${s.asset}" aria-hidden="true"></div>

      <div class="glyph b lm-${s.asset}" aria-hidden="true"></div>

    </div>

    <div class="sec-copy">

      <span class="eyebrow">${s.eyebrow}</span>

      <p>${s.copy}</p>

    </div>`;

  main.appendChild(sec);

});


/* ---------------- nav / overlays ---------------- */

document.querySelectorAll("[data-anchor]").forEach(a=>a.addEventListener("click",e=>{

  e.preventDefault();

  document.querySelector(a.getAttribute("href")).scrollIntoView({behavior:"smooth"});

}));

document.querySelectorAll("[data-overlay]").forEach(btn=>{

  btn.addEventListener("click",()=>{

    const ov = document.getElementById("ov-"+btn.dataset.overlay);

    const r = btn.getBoundingClientRect();

    const ox=(r.left+r.width/2)+"px", oy=(r.top+r.height/2)+"px";

    ov.dataset.ox=ox; ov.dataset.oy=oy;

    ov.style.visibility="visible";

    gsap.fromTo(ov,{clipPath:`circle(0% at ${ox} ${oy})`},

      {clipPath:`circle(150% at ${ox} ${oy})`,duration:.7,ease:"power3.inOut"});

    ov.querySelector(".close").focus();

  });

});

document.querySelectorAll("[data-close]").forEach(btn=>{

  btn.addEventListener("click",()=>{

    const ov = btn.closest(".overlay");

    gsap.to(ov,{clipPath:`circle(0% at ${ov.dataset.ox} ${ov.dataset.oy})`,

      duration:.5,ease:"power3.inOut",onComplete:()=>ov.style.visibility="hidden"});

  });

});


/* ---------------- motion ---------------- */

const mm = gsap.matchMedia();

mm.add({

  full:"(prefers-reduced-motion: no-preference) and (min-width: 769px)",

  mobile:"(prefers-reduced-motion: no-preference) and (max-width: 768px)",

  reduced:"(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)"

},(ctx)=>{

  const {full, mobile, reduced} = ctx.conditions;


  if(reduced){ document.body.classList.add("rm"); return; }


  /* hero intro — quick, skippable */

  const intro = gsap.timeline({defaults:{ease:"power3.out"}});

  intro

    .from("#heroMark",{scale:.86,opacity:0,duration:1.2},0)

    .from("nav",{opacity:0,duration:.6},.7)

    .from(".hero-cue",{opacity:0,duration:.6},1.0);

  const skip=()=>{ if(intro.progress()<1) intro.progress(1); };

  window.addEventListener("wheel",skip,{once:true,passive:true});

  window.addEventListener("touchstart",skip,{once:true,passive:true});


  /* hero scroll-out: lockup recedes into the black */

  gsap.to("#heroLockup",{scale:.9,opacity:0,ease:"none",

    scrollTrigger:{trigger:".hero",start:"top top",end:"85% top",scrub:true}});


  /* letter sections */

  gsap.utils.toArray(".letter-section").forEach((sec,i)=>{

    const axis = SECTIONS[i].axis;

    const v = mobile ? {r:{x:"-70vw",y:0,rot:0}, b:{x:"70vw",y:0,rot:0}} : vectors(axis);

    const r = sec.querySelector(".glyph.r");

    const b = sec.querySelector(".glyph.b");

    const depth = sec.querySelector(".bg-depth");

    const copy = sec.querySelector(".sec-copy");

    const scaleIn = mobile ? 1.6 : 2.6;


    const tl = gsap.timeline({

      scrollTrigger:{

        trigger:sec, start:"top top",

        end: mobile ? "+=160%" : "+=220%",

        pin:true, scrub:0.6, anticipatePin:1

      }

    });


    /* ENTER: huge, off-screen, transparent at the very edge */

    tl.fromTo(r,

      {xPercent:-50,yPercent:-50,x:v.r.x,y:v.r.y,rotation:v.r.rot,scale:scaleIn,opacity:0},

      {opacity:1,duration:.06,ease:"none"},0)

      .to(r,{x:mobile?0:"3vw",y:0,rotation:0,scale:1.12,duration:.4,ease:"power2.in"},0)

      .to(r,{x:0,scale:1,duration:.14,ease:"power3.out"},.4);

    tl.fromTo(b,

      {xPercent:-50,yPercent:-50,x:v.b.x,y:v.b.y,rotation:v.b.rot,scale:scaleIn,opacity:0},

      {opacity:1,duration:.06,ease:"none"},0)

      .to(b,{x:mobile?0:"-3vw",y:0,rotation:0,scale:1.12,duration:.4,ease:"power2.in"},0)

      .to(b,{x:0,scale:1,duration:.14,ease:"power3.out"},.4);


    /* HOLD: merged magenta, copy reads (0.54 → 0.78) */

    tl.from(copy,{y:34,opacity:0,duration:.16,ease:"power2.out"},.5);


    /* EXIT: scale up and leave the frame as pin releases */

    tl.to([r,b],{scale:2.4,y:"-70vh",opacity:0,duration:.22,ease:"power2.in"},.78)

      .to(copy,{opacity:0,y:-20,duration:.12},.82);


    /* the channel: laid-back giant letter drifts slower than scroll */

    gsap.fromTo(depth,

      {rotateX:62,yPercent:8},

      {yPercent:-10,ease:"none",

       scrollTrigger:{trigger:sec,start:"top bottom",end:"bottom top",scrub:true}});

  });


  /* divisions */

  if(full){

    gsap.fromTo("#panelLeft",{clipPath:"inset(0 0 0 100%)"},{clipPath:"inset(0 0 0 0%)",ease:"power3.out",

      scrollTrigger:{trigger:"#divisions",start:"top 70%",end:"top 20%",scrub:true}});

    gsap.fromTo("#panelRight",{clipPath:"inset(0 100% 0 0)"},{clipPath:"inset(0 0% 0 0)",ease:"power3.out",

      scrollTrigger:{trigger:"#divisions",start:"top 70%",end:"top 20%",scrub:true}});

  }else{

    gsap.from(".div-panel",{y:60,opacity:0,stagger:.15,

      scrollTrigger:{trigger:"#divisions",start:"top 75%"}});

  }


  gsap.from("footer .big",{y:50,opacity:0,duration:.8,ease:"power3.out",

    scrollTrigger:{trigger:"footer",start:"top 75%"}});

});

</script>

</body>

</html>
